        function onTitleClick(NsaVal) {
            document.getElementById('ctl00_MainContent_hdnServiceName').value = NsaVal;
        }

        function ShowHistory(id) {
            if (null != document.getElementById(id)) {
                document.getElementById(id).style.display = 'block';
            }
        }

        function HideHistory(id) {
            if (null != document.getElementById(id)) {
                document.getElementById(id).style.display = 'none';
            }
        }

        function ShowHistory1(id) {
            document.getElementById(id).style.display = 'block';
        }

        function HidePanel() {
            // For Hiding the Panel inside "gvStatusToday" Grid
            if (document.getElementById("ctl00_MainContent_gvStatusToday") != null) {
                var cntTrArr = document.getElementById("ctl00_MainContent_gvStatusToday").children[0].children;
                var childcount = cntTrArr.length;
                var digit = '0';
                if (childcount > 0) {
                    for (var i = 0; i < childcount - 1; i++) {
                        if (i >= 8) {
                            digit = '';
                        }
                        element = document.getElementById('ctl00_MainContent_gvStatusToday_ctl' + digit + (i + 2) + '_Panel1');
                        element.style.display = 'none';
                        if (element.childNodes.length <= 1) {
                            element.style.border = 'none';
                            element.style.borderBottom = 'none';
                        }

                    }

                }
            }

            if (document.getElementById("ctl00_MainContent_gvStatusToday") != null) {
                var cntTrArr = document.getElementById("ctl00_MainContent_gvStatusToday").children[0].children;
                var childcount = cntTrArr.length;
                var digit = '0';
                if (childcount > 0) {
                    for (var i = 0; i < childcount - 1; i++) {
                        if (i >= 8) {
                            digit = '';
                        }
                        element = document.getElementById('ctl00_MainContent_gvStatusToday_ctl' + digit + (i + 2) + '_Panel2');
                        element.style.display = 'none';
                        if (element.childNodes.length <= 1) {
                            element.style.border = 'none';
                            element.style.borderBottom = 'none';
                        }

                    }

                }
            }

            // For Hiding the Panel inside "gvStatusToday" Grid
            for (var panelCount = 2; panelCount < 9; panelCount++) {
                if (document.getElementById("ctl00_MainContent_GridViewHistory") != null) {
                    var cntTrArr = document.getElementById("ctl00_MainContent_GridViewHistory").children[0].children;
                    var childcount = cntTrArr.length;
                    var digit = '0';
                    if (childcount > 0) {
                        for (var i = 0; i < childcount - 1; i++) {
                            if (i >= 8) {
                                digit = '';
                            }
                            element = document.getElementById('ctl00_MainContent_GridViewHistory_ctl' + digit + (i + 2) + '_Panel' + panelCount);
                            element.style.display = 'none';
                            if (element.childNodes.length <= 1) {
                                element.style.border = 'none';
                                element.style.borderBottom = 'none';
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }

        function test() {

        }

        function reportIssueRedirect(id) {
            if (parent.document) {
                parent.document.location.href = document.getElementById('ctl00_MainContent_hdnReportIssueUrl').value;
            }
            else {
                document.location.href = document.getElementById('ctl00_MainContent_hdnReportIssueUrl').value;
            }
        }
